Prologue

The explosions echoed loudly. Black smoke billowed, and the smell of burning flesh filled the air. The stone walls came crumbling down as the castle town was enveloped in a sea of flames. Within the red-stained sky hovered several black dots. One of them abruptly descended at incredible speed, shaking the ground as it crash-landed. What was revealed to be a monster then opened a gigantic maw lined with razor-sharp teeth and breathed a stream of flames all around. Men and women who were running about screaming in panic were reduced to mere ashes in the blink of an eye. A child crying for his mother suddenly found himself picked up by a huge hand. The owner of the hand, a giant who towered over all the nearby houses, opened its mouth to bite off his head. Just in the nick of time, someone chopped off the hand holding the child.

"Everything's gonna be fine! Now that I've arrived, I won't allow the monsters to do as they please any longer!"

"It's the Hero! It's the Hero, Takayuki!"

Hope reignited in the eyes of the people who had been simply running about aimlessly a moment ago. Immediately afterwards, fire magic slammed into the giant's face. The giant brought its hands to its face and roared, even while turning into smoke. A beautiful woman holding a staff encrusted with gems appeared behind the Hero, followed by a blonde woman carrying a huge sword.

"The Holy Maiden and the Holy Dame are also here! We're saved!"

The gathering crowd pumped their fists into the air. This man had been summoned from another world using all of the resources at the kingdom's disposal. He and his companions were surely going to save this country - nay, this entire world. Everyone present believed this with all their heart, and they cheered to express it. A roar of defiance rose up from within the dancing, crimson flames. Splat.

"Eh?"

However, that roar was cut short almost as soon as it began. Above the heads of the Hero and his companions, who were waving in response to the cheering, fell several boulders twice the size of a carriage. These three heroes, upon whose shoulders rode the hope of retaliation, were squashed flat like inconsequential insects.

Everything had happened so suddenly that the onlookers were dumbstruck, their jaws hanging open and their fists still in the air. The Hero's party was not supposed to die. Any moment now the boulder was going to crack into pieces, and they would emerge unscathed...was surely what many of those present had been thinking. However, a red liquid oozed out from underneath the boulders. This was the cruel reality.

"The Hero... The great Hero has..."

"We...we're doomed!!"

All that was left after the silence was tragedy. Every single person - be they man or woman, old or young - fell into the stomachs of monsters one by one. Everything that lived and breathed was massacred without mercy.

The farce that had just taken place evoked a sigh from a woman who had been watching from her vantage point on top of a hill that overlooked the town. Then again, everyone else together with her on the hill had also been watching, so it wasn't as if she were the only one.

"So that just now was the self-proclaimed 'Hero' who had been called from another world using a large summoning spell? For someone who claimed that 'I can save you all because I was granted a special power when I came to this world,' he didn't do all that much fighting."

"They are fools, every last one of them. What would be the point of hard work if it was so easy to get strong? Even the tiniest scrap of growth is attained only with incremental effort, ingeniosity, dedication, and a staggering amount of time. Why do they not understand this?"

"I agree. Humans really are stupid. Just because they know how to cooperate with each other and use tools and devise strategies, they think themselves hot stuff. Even monsters have the ability to think for themselves and make discoveries and invent things."

Feeling resigned, the woman listened to the mocking going on behind her with only half an ear. Although she had no recollection of it, she was sure that she had seen these two sights many times before: foolish humans pushing their problems onto unrelated strangers instead of trying to resolve things with their own strength and then paying the price for such inanity, and so-called "Heroes" getting carried away with all the flattery and dying a dog's death. The woman's memories no longer remained, but her feelings did.

"Well then... I suppose we should get down there as well. We've probably had this exact same conversation countless times before, but even so, we can't very well continue watching this tragedy without doing anything," said an old man with a muscular body, stepping forward while rubbing his goatee.

The figures behind him, which numbered slightly over a hundred, followed suit. Everyone here came from the same place and were in the same position as the woman. Back when monsters first appeared in this world, they, too, had also appeared at the same time. The task that they had been entrusted with was simple: to fight, down to the very last person, so that just one more resident of this world could live for just one more second. Despite knowing that everything and everyone was slated for death, these individuals still had to fulfill their duty.

After everything, it looks like this world is going the same way. Once more, we will be reabsorbed, purified, and manifested. Again and again and again...just the same cycle going on for what's probably eternity. Will we never get to rest...?

The woman shook her head to bring herself out of her thoughts. She drew the kunai from her waist, then took off together with the rest of the crowd. While pumping her legs, she lifted up a prayer that she had probably made countless times before.

Someone, please, stop this cycle. I've probably placed my hopes on the next iteration again and again. Even so, I pray. I pray that next time, a true Hero will finally appear who will stop this nightmare from repeating itself yet again...

Chapter 1: Dungeon System Activation

Of the Twenty-Three Special Wards of Tokyo, Edogawa City - the wards called themselves "cities" - ranked pretty much at the top, right next to Adachi City for being "the least desirable city to live in." The general image held by those not living there was that it was a place that, due to being frequented by delinquents even in this day and age, had very bad public order. The truth of the matter, however, was that it was an extremely liveable city. This was especially true of the area alongside the Toei Shinjuku Line between Funabori Station and Mizue Station, a neighborhood within which could be found multiple supermarkets and no shortage of public facilities, like parks and sports centers. To top it off, rent here was extremely reasonable. Because of all these reasons, there was even a certain percentage of the population who were born here, worked here, and planned to die here as well. In a way, I, too, was one of them.

I, Ezoe Kazuhiko, am a resident of Edogawa City and am turning forty this year. If asked what I did for a living, I'd say management consulting. It was ten years ago that I obtained my Small and Medium Enterprise Management Consultant license and quit my job. Now, I make my living taking on jobs related to social insurance from small and medium companies in the area around Edogawa City, Koto City, and Chiba Prefecture, with the occasional lecturer gig at a training course. It might sound like I do a lot, but my annual income never really exceeded the six-million mark.

Having no intention of getting married, I had bought a modest, thirtyyear-old house located in the Shishibone neighborhood, a place so lonely - even for Edogawa City - that it had earned the nickname of "Landbound Solitary Island." Out of the seven days of the week, I would work two days, rest a day, work two more days, then rest the remaining two days. Mine was a laid-back lifestyle with three days off weekly..

I had no siblings, and both my parents had already passed away. I did have a few slightly removed relatives living not too far away who would come over every once in a while, but that was about it. I knew quite a few people in the area, but there were only a small handful who I considered close friends. There was no one to order me about and no one that I had to always be considerate towards. Despite not being all that affluent, life was still enjoyable and stress free.

"Hey there, Ezoe-san. How you doin'? You feel like dropping by tonight?"

One of the advantages of the bachelor lifestyle was the freedom to go drink wherever and whenever without having to mind anyone else. Not too far away from the northern entrance of Mizue Station was one of my favorite lounges, ROCO. It was one of the staff members, Mochizuki, who had called out to me.

"Who's there tonight, Mocchii?"

"It's Yuzu-san tonight."

"Sure, count me in, then."

In this way, I would drop by this place about once every week. As a selfemployed bachelor, weekdays and weekends were all the same to me. When I felt like drinking, I drank; when I felt like sleeping, I slept. What I had attained after being freed from the bindings of company life was overwhelming freedom. After drinking for about two hours, I took a taxi home.

Shishibone, the area where I lived, was a large "railway blindspot" sandwiched between Mizue Station on the Toei Shinjuku Line and Koiwa Station of the Sobu Line. The distance from where I lived to either of those stations was roughly a thirty minutes' walk. My fifty-square-meter plot of land had a second-hand, detached house and a small yard. Here was where I planned to live out the rest of my quiet, modest life.

I took off my jacket and retrieved a beer from the fridge. As I was also feeling a bit peckish, I poured hot water in one of the cup noodles that I had in stock. It was already past midnight, but tomorrow was one of my planned days off, so it didn't matter if I stayed up late. Lately, I had been growing a bit of a belly, and my blood pressure levels were starting to climb a little. But what was one more night? I felt a slight tremor or wobble, probably because of all the alcohol in me. After kicking my slacks off as well - which reduced me to my trunks - I then added super-spicy sauce to my favorite flavor of seafood noodles and ate it. In the end, it was way past 2 a.m. when I finally went to bed.

In my own way, I was happy with my routine-like life of basically a stable sameness sprinkled with the occasional bit of excitement.

"What...is this hole...?"

Or at least, I was happy, up until that fateful day at the end of June, when the name of Japan's new era had only just been ushered in.

◇ ◇ ◇

The slight tremor that I had felt last night had already completely left my mind. After waking up at 9 a.m., I started the washing machine and ate a simple breakfast while waiting. When I went outside afterwards to hang out the freshly washed load, I noticed a square hole in a corner of my yard that looked roughly one meter long on each side. I tilted my head in puzzlement. Wondering what it was, I lit it up with a flashlight and discovered a flight of stone steps that led underground.

"An underground room? I don't remember hearing about this when I bought the house."

My wristwatch indicated that it was 9:55 a.m. Both today and tomorrow were days off on my schedule, which meant I had nothing planned. With a flashlight and an oil lighter in hand, I gingerly descended the stairs. Judging by the direction, it led underneath the neighboring plot. As much as possible, I wanted to avoid trouble with my neighbors. While considering whether I should seal this hole with two-by-fours, I carefully continued down. The lighter in my hand remained lit, from which I gathered that I didn't have to worry about oxygen.

"...This is really deep. How far does it go?"

By feel, I determined that I had descended roughly the height of a tenstory apartment building by the time I finally reached the bottom. I heaved a small sigh of relief at the sensation of my feet on flat ground again, then turned around to look at the flight of stairs that I'd just come down. It was a lot steeper than I'd thought. Just thinking about having to climb all the way back up to get out was enough to make me feel down.

"This underground area is pretty spacious. If I put in a bit of time and effort, I might be able to use it for something."

Pointing my flashlight in all four directions and up and down, I gauged the space to be about fifteen meters on each of the four sides with a clearance of more than three meters. The floor was paved with stone but with absolutely no gaps whatsoever between the paving. As I continued looking around, I noticed the wall in front of me reflecting the light of my flashlight.

"A...door?"

There before my eyes were sturdy-looking double doors with a metallic sheen that towered more than two meters high. I hadn't noticed it earlier due to its black coating.

"A bomb shelter? Or an abandoned military facility from WWII?"

There were no weld marks between the metallic doorknob and the door, almost as if it was all one, single piece. Thinking that it would probably be a good idea to check out the inside first before reporting this to my local government office, I grabbed the doorknob. That instant, a voice suddenly rang out.

First Contacter confirmed. In accordance with World Order, hereby activating the Dungeon System. ETA to the activation of all dungeons: one revolution.

"Wh-What?! Where did that voice come from?!"

The cold, robotic voice was surprisingly loud, causing me to clasp my hands over my ears. However, that did nothing to decrease its volume. It was almost as if the voice was speaking directly inside my head.

As the reward, you are hereby granted the Character Card "Akane the Glamorous Kunoichi," the lifting of your card possession limit, expansion of your skill slots, and the authority to choose your skills. Native ability "Card

Gacha" has been installed.

"Huh? Kunoichi as in a female ninja? Card? What card?"

Dungeon Roulette has been spun. Fixed coordinates confirmed. Dungeon name: Abyss. Difficulty: A. Drop rewards: A. Available Enhancement Element: A. Congratulations. We look forward to your progress towards a new transformation.

The strange voice cut off as suddenly as it had started. Before my eyes was a single, glowing card floating in midair.

"What...is this?"

The mysterious underground room that had appeared all of a sudden, the strange doors, and the voice that had almost given me a headache and its incomprehensible message had left me so bewildered that I did not have the mental capacity to worry about the impossibility of something floating in midair by itself. As the card was glowing on its own, I didn't even have to direct my flashlight at it.

Before reaching out for it, I carefully studied the card. On its surface was such a realistic depiction of a person that it almost looked like a photograph. A black-haired woman in what appeared to be a ninja outfit was posing with a kunai - that's what those small ninja daggers are called, right? - in hand. My general impression was that this looked like a card from a card game.

Slowly, I reached forward and grasped the card. It felt rather strange to the touch. Despite being as hard as a plate of metal, the surface felt matte. I flipped it over and found words written on the back. It was in Japanese.

-------------------------------------------------------------------

Name: Akane

Title: Glamorous Kunoichi

Rank: F

Rarity: Legend Rare

Skills: Kunai Mastery (Lvl. 1), Enemy Detection (Lvl. 1), Sex Technique

(Lvl. 1)

-------------------------------------------------------------------

"Akane...Glamorous Kunoichi? Let's see. What's this bottom part say? 'An all-rounder character capable of close quarters combat using a kunai or dagger, long-range combat using projectiles like the shuriken, and other ninja techniques such as enemy detection. Also proficient at sex techniques to provide enjoyment while resting.' Height of 163 centimeters, Bust 99, Waist

57, Hips 87..."

As I continued reading out loud, the light of the card continued growing stronger until it got so bright that I had to let the card go and turn my face away. Several moments later, the light subsided, leaving me in darkness.

"Oh my. Are you my Master?"

"UWAAAH!"

A voice suddenly addressed me from within the darkness. It wasn't a voice inside my head but a real voice. When I pointed my flashlight in the direction of the voice, I found a black-haired beauty with a bewitching smile on her face.

"What a crude thing to point at a woman."

In a split second, the woman had snatched away my flashlight and turned it off. The room became entirely enveloped in darkness.

"Don't worry. The Safety Zone of Floor 1 should be activating soon."

"Just who are you...?" I asked nervously towards the part of the darkness where I thought the woman was. There was a faint fragrance of flowers in the air. After a short while, my eyes gradually got used to the darkness, allowing me to once again make out the figure of my companion. Then it struck me: the floor, ceiling, and walls were luminescing. Before long, the room became brightly lit with a soft light. The beauty bowed gracefully.

"It is my pleasure meeting you, my Master. I am the kunoichi Akane."

"Akane-...san. Oh, sorry, I'm Ezoe Kazuhiko. Honestly, I still haven't the faintest idea what's going on, and my head's a jumble."

Even while answering, my eyes were glued to the woman's body. The upper part of her body was covered by what looked like chainmail with very fine mesh, on top of which she also had on jet-black clothing. On her lower half, she was wearing something similar to a Chinese-style dress - for ease of movement, maybe? - the kind with slits on both sides that revealed her slender and voluptuous bare legs. What caught my attention the most was her chest. With the chainmail sticking close, her two very shapely breasts stood out like gigantic meat buns.

She giggled sexily. "I sense a lascivious gaze."

"S-Sorry," I replied while turning my face away. The very pleasant aroma emanating from the glamorous woman tickled my nose.

"I don't mind. I am, after all, your servant. Every single inch of this body is yours, Master. I also possess knowledge of how to pleasure men. Feel free to do whatever you wish to me."

"Uh, that's not quite..."

Abruptly, I felt a breath blown into my ear. I jumped backwards in a fluster as my head whipped around. There stood Akane-san with a graceful smile on her face.

"Have you calmed down yet?"

Finally, I realized that she had been teasing me. I heaved a huge sigh. To her credit, however, I had indeed calmed down. When someone's mind is locked in a state of confusion, making them think about something else is an effective way to bring them out of it. Having regained my presence of mind, I proceeded to sort out the information I had on hand.

"I'm sorry, but give me a minute."

My footsteps rang out as I paced around the stone-paved room. I combed through the little bit of information that I already knew to determine what I was still missing and consolidate my preliminary analysis of what this place was.

This underground space that appeared out of the blue, the strange voice and the incomprehensible things it said, the shining card, and the woman before me... What I should draw from all of that is...

Roughly sixty seconds later, my feet stopped.

"You...no, Akane-san. I have a question. Exactly what is the Dungeon System?"

The beautiful woman licked her lips with her pale-pink tongue.

◇ ◇ ◇

I, Akane, am one of the 108 Stars of Destiny incorporated into the Dungeon System. If I were to be honest, when I first laid eyes on Master, I had felt disappointment welling inside. His middle-aged and slightly chubby appearance did not look strong at all, and neither did I feel the attractiveness of a man from him. On top of all that, he had sent a lewd look towards my breasts almost the moment he laid eyes on me. If he had assaulted me at that moment, I would have summarily beheaded him. Us Stars of Destiny had the special right to choose our Masters.

"S-Sorry," he said while turning around. As it turned out, he wasn't someone who would act solely based on desire. He looked very confused, and so I decided to lend a hand helping him calm down. I was willing to comfort him with my hands, but apparently I did not need to go so far.

"I'm sorry, but give me a minute."

After being ordered so, I fell silent and observed my new Master. Having calmed down, the light of intelligence gleamed in his eyes. I could tell that he was furiously sorting through information inside his head. In other words, on top of possessing the reasoning to suppress his instincts, he also had the acumen to analyze a situation. Though he seemed a bit lacking in ardor, at the very least, he didn't seem like a bad Master. With the Dungeon System having been activated, this world had begun the march towards obliteration. If he displayed the will and determination to stand up in the face of this hopeless future, then I was willing to consider offering him my body. Oh, it looks like he's finished his contemplation. Well then, what will his first question be?

◇ ◇ ◇

I was aware that I was not dreaming. The situation was incomprehensible, and so I had to start by sorting through what I did comprehend. At times like these, wondering "why" was not helpful, as there usually wasn't an answer. While recalling the robotic voice from earlier, I mapped out the pieces of information inside my head and determined their respective priority levels. After all this, the most important-sounding keyword naturally floated to the top.

"Exactly what is the Dungeon System?"

"The Dungeon System is a part of the natural law of this universe, which also goes by the name of 'World Order.' No one knows the reason for the System's existence nor its aim. Please just think of it as a natural phenomenon, just as how water flows from high to low."

To sum up what Akane-san then said, these spaces called "dungeons" that existed in a different space or dimension had begun appearing in our world for an unknown reason.

"In the next year, an additional 665 dungeons will gradually appear, spread out over ten waves of sixty-five or sixty-six each. As dungeons are drawn to people, all of them should be appearing in places where large numbers of people are gathered."

"Right, so that's why the voice mentioned 'one revolution.' Moving on. I will now go over what my understanding is. If any part of it is wrong or if you are able to elaborate in any way, then please let me know. When I hear 'dungeon,' I think of a gigantic cave filled with ferocious monsters that assault humans. Is this the case here?"

Even though I did not play computer games, I wasn't entirely unfamiliar with the word "dungeon" in the gaming sense. At the very least, I knew that this was a word commonly associated with the fantasy genre, with one example being the "Something Quest" game that had been a huge hit around thirty years ago.

Akane-san nodded in response to my question. "That is correct. The only difference is that these are not caves but other dimensions."

"I see. Leaving the thing about other dimensions aside for now, please tell me what you know about these dungeons. For example, if I killed one of the monsters inside, would I get anything? It's the characteristics and rules of the

dungeons that I want to know most right now."

"As you wish, Master." Akane-san bowed. "Then allow me to share my knowledge. First, I shall go over the difficulty ranking of the dungeons. The lowest difficulty is D, and the highest is S. There are only seven Rank S dungeons. The next difficulty, A, takes up around 10% of the total number, which means there are anywhere from sixty to seventy of them. B and C make up the bulk of the dungeons at around 70% of the total, leaving the last rank, D, at around 20%. Each dungeon's ranking is determined by its number of floors and the strength of the monsters that appear inside. However, not all dungeons within the same tier are alike. For example, there are Rank B dungeons closer to being Rank A, Rank C dungeons closer to being Rank B, and so on. Additionally, a dungeon's ranking is also greatly affected by the kinds of rewards that it generates."

"I want to hear more about specifically what kinds of rewards there are. Would they be 'magic stones' or 'monster materials' like the genre commonly posits, or are they something else entirely?"

"There are indeed such cases, but for civilized societies, the most common reward would be money."

"I'm sorry, what?"

Money? If I defeat a monster, a Yukichi would appear? For a split second, my mind ground to a halt.

"The general criteria that dungeons use when deciding rewards is 'something that is of value to the world that they have appeared in.' In some worlds, that would be food, water, air, or any other number of things. However, for civilizations that have progressed to the point where they understand the concept of 'money,' that becomes the default reward most of

the time. That said, there are exceptions, too, of course."

The development often described in light novels, where the fact that killing monsters yields money leaks and incites mobs of civilians to flood into the dungeons to strike it rich, was very much not what I was imagining. If a cash-generating dungeon appeared, the government would definitely step in. Currency issuance was an economic policy. How much money was printed would affect employment rates, the prices of commodities, and exchange rates. There was no way that a country would just open up a dungeon that would be pumping unknown amounts of cash into the economy.

"If the Dungeon System thinks that it could attract people to enter the dungeons by generating money, then it is a defective system. There is no way that countries would leave these dungeons be. Without a doubt, countries would move to clamp down on them, instead sending their police force or their armies inside to shut them down. Not that I know how effective automatic rifles would be against monsters..."

"The Dungeon System grants autonomous control to the dungeons, such that it could be said that each dungeon is an entity with the ability to think for itself, decide what kinds of monsters it contains, and what rewards it generates. As such, it is very possible for rewards other than money to be dropped. However, what you mentioned about sending in armies to shut down the dungeons would most likely not work. After all, it is impossible to bring outside weapons into a dungeon."

"Hm? What do you mean? Weapons can't be brought in?"

"Yes, that is correct. So now we get to the most important part of the

System. I shall now explain about the cards."

Akane-san drew one of the kunai from her waist, then showed it to me.

Abruptly, the kunai turned into a card. It looked like a sleight of hand trick.

"This is no trickery. It is a part of the Dungeon System. When I said that it is impossible to bring weapons into a dungeon, it is because anything that the dungeon determines to be a weapon would be converted into a card just like so. In order to restore a cardified weapon, it needs to be brought back to the

'Safety Zone' that is located at the entrance at Floor 1."

"If weapons can't be brought in, then how are we supposed to fight inside the dungeons?"

"There are two ways. One way is for you to acquire weapons inside the dungeon and fight in person. The other way is to order servants - such as myself - to fight on your behalf. There is no other way. If you choose the first, you will have to first start out fighting with only your bare fists, gradually proceeding deeper in until you find a weapon. The only weapons that can be brought into a dungeon are 'dungeon-made' ones."

"I see. And the 'servant' that you mentioned as the other way?"

"When monsters in a dungeon are defeated, there is a chance for them to turn into a card that can then be picked up. These are 'servants.' Servants can be summoned only inside of dungeons. Once summoned, they can be ordered to fight on their Master's behalf. There are a few other ways of obtaining cards, such as by freeing spirits that had been sealed away or by dealing with

Peddler, an otherworldly merchant who wanders throughout the dungeons."

"I see. So it's basically a choice between becoming a fighter or a summoner. So then, what about you? Why are you here, even though I haven't done any fighting yet?"

"Master, you are the first person who has come into contact with the Dungeon System. As the reward for being the First Contacter, I believe you must have received several perks. Please say 'Status Open' out loud."

"Uh... Status Open."

Abruptly, a black screen roughly fifty centimeters tall and thirty centimeters wide appeared before my eyes. There were white words on the screen.

-------------------------------------------------------------------

Name: Ezoe Kazuhiko

Title: First Contacter

Rank: F

Possession Limit: 0 / ∞

Skills: Card Gacha, ______, ______, ______, ______, ______

-------------------------------------------------------------------

Akane-san giggled. "As expected of the First Contacter. Your possession limit is infinite, and you have six skill slots."

"You can see this? And by 'possession limit,' you mean card possession limit? Your surprise at me having six skill slots means...?"

"First, this is the Status screen. You can only call it out when inside a dungeon. It is indeed visible to everyone else, so be careful about checking it when there are others around. Next, the possession limit. This is the maximum number of cards that you can have in your possession while inside a dungeon. For normal people, this is capped around twenty to thirty. Due to the reward you received, this limit has effectively been lifted for you. Then lastly, about the skill slots. Normal people only have two or three slots, whereas you have six. This skill that you already possess, 'Card Gacha,' is not something that I am familiar with..."

"Uhhh...'gacha' refers to a loot box system - I think that's what the kids call it nowadays? - inside video games where things like items and characters can be obtained through a random selec- You know what, don't worry about it. I think I have a pretty good idea what it is. Back to the possession limit. My Status is showing '0' at the moment. Are you not being counted?"

"That is because I am currently materialized and also due to the fact that I am a Legend Rare card, the very rarest kind. When you enter the dungeon, you will attain monster cards. Do you wish to try entering now?"

"No, I will need to make preparations first. I'll listen to the rest of what you have to say in my house. Let's go up for now," I said while turning towards the stairs.

However, Akane-san made no move to follow me. When I turned around, she sighed softly and said apologetically, "As I have just mentioned, servants can only be summoned within dungeons. As soon as I attempt to leave, I will become cardified. You will be able to converse with me only when down here."

"I see. Is there any penalty or cost for summoning you?" "Not particularly, no..."

"Then I'm sorry, but can you turn back into a card for me? I want to put down everything that's happened on paper. And more importantly, I've been wanting to go to the toilet for a while now."

"As you wish. And one last thing: please call me 'Akane' without any honorifics. You are my Master, and I am your servant, so you adding '-san' to my name confounds me."

"Very well. Then you can also stop calling me 'Master.' Call me by my last name or first name. Being called 'Master' confounds me."

"Your wish is my command, Kazuhiko-sama."

Right when I was about to object to the '-sama' suffix, Akane turned into a card with a small 'poof.' This time, her card fell straight to the ground without floating in midair. I picked it up in a fluster, then put it away in my chest pocket.

◇ ◇ ◇

It was after I had finished my business in the toilet and was enjoying a puff under the ventilation fan that a realization hit me. According to my smartphone, the time was only just past 10 a.m. Feeling puzzled, I checked my wristwatch. By my rough estimate, I had spent around twenty minutes checking out the dungeon and talking to Akane. And true enough, the wristwatch that I had been wearing when going down there was indicating 10:30 a.m.

"What does this mean? Is my watch broken? Or could it be..." I unconsciously brought a hand over my mouth. "...that the flow of time is different?"

Without further ado, I immediately proceeded to test my theory. I prepared two quartz watches, put one of them on, and tied the other to a spool of kite string. After confirming that the two were synchronized, I lowered the latter while observing from aboveground. As I had half expected, the second hand started spinning as if out of control. I quickly pulled it back up and once again reset the time. This time, I lowered it even deeper and waited a full minute before retrieving it once more. Lo and behold, despite having started off at 0:00, the watch was now off by about two hours. Through this experiment, I was now fully convinced that time inside the dungeon passed faster than outside.

"I'm going to need to ask Akane about this, just in case."

Resolving myself to the fate of muscle soreness, I once again descended the stairs that led underground.

"Six rolls, for which I get four Cs and two UCs. Rough estimate would be 80% C and 20% UC then. Next time, let's do an eleven-roll with monster cards from Floor 2. If the distribution is still the same, then it can be concluded that Card Gacha's cost return is just bad, period. If not, then my hypothesis becomes substantiated. That aside, what's this last item?"

I materialized the last item that I'd gotten from Item Gacha, the "Time Stop Barrier." When I turned to Akane, it turned out that she was familiar with it.

"This is an item used by knight orders and armies as they clear dungeons. You stick these small talismans all over the Safety Zone, then also stick this activation talisman when you leave. When this barrier is activated, time inside the Safety Zone is stopped. This helps prevent water and foodstuffs from getting stale or going bad."

"How wonderful! This would be enormously helpful. But then why is such a useful item only ranked as UC?"

"Kazuhiko-sama, who do you imagine would be able to take advantage of this item?"

It was from Akane's reminder that it occurred to me: stopping time inside

a Safety Zone means monopolizing the dungeon. On the other hand, the general dungeon would usually see an unspecified number of people coming and going. In other words, this item can only be used by someone with complete control over a dungeon.

"Aside from organizations such as knight orders and armies who are clearing a dungeon, say, based on an imperial edict from their emperor, this item is useless to most everyone else. That is likely why its rarity is so low."

This dungeon, however, was different. As its entrance was in my yard, I already had sole control over it by default. I decided to test this item out immediately.

"So I first stick these little pieces of parchment in the corners of the room...then above the entrance that leads aboveground, right there. Using extra-strong adhesive to weather the faster time progression down here..."

As soon as I had finished putting all the talismans up, I tried activating it immediately. Right before stepping out, I had Akane flip a five hundred yen coin. Then I quickly moved my foot away and activated the barrier. From the stairs, I saw both Akane and the coin frozen like a painting.

"It worked. Let's go back in."

I immediately turned around and reentered the Safety Zone, at which the five hundred yen coin landed on the ground normally as if nothing had happened. Akane asked me how it went.

"It was a success. Thanks to this, I can now remodel the Safety Zone even further. First would be a bed. Let's get a luxury mattress, the one used by sports athletes. While I'm at it, I could also consider getting batteries with even higher capacities. I think I remember seeing portable five-thousand-watt ones before."

"So finally you will be bringing proper bedding down! My first night with Kazuhiko-sama...rather than the flimsy one over there, I would much prefer doing it on proper sheets!"

As Akane sidled up with me with a blush on her cheeks, I responded with a vague "Mm, eventually." Then I turned back towards the cards that were still laid out over the desk.

"I will need to use a weapon on Floor 2. I suppose the spear makes the most sense. Are there any of these that you want, Akane?"

"If I may, I would like the kunai and one of the daggers. What I had on hand was sufficient for Floor 1, but I will very likely need spare weapons for what's coming."

"That makes sense. All right then, I'll be taking this spear. And as a backup, the remaining dagger. The leftover club...well, I'll just put it away for now."

When I handed the Kunai Card and one of the Dagger Cards to Akane, she materialized both of them with small poofs, examined them closely, then nodded in satisfaction. I materialized the steel spear to test out how it felt. Just as the description had mentioned, it did feel a bit heavy. Around five kilograms, I think?

"I see, so the handle part is hollow inside. Well, if the whole thing was a solid steel pipe, then it would be too heavy to use."

"When you reach Rank D, you will become capable of brandishing even heavier weapons without any issue, so the weight is not so much an issue. What I believe to be more important, rather, is learning how to wield the spear."

"Ahhh, good point. Guess I'll pull something up from a video-hosting site. However - and I don't mean to underestimate the importance of technique - strengthening my body takes higher priority for now. I've gotten quite a lot thinner..."

"You look wonderful, Kazuhiko-sama."

My chin, which had been quite flabby half a month ago, was now very sharp. Much of the extra fat on my cheeks, back, and around my stomach had also fallen off. If I flexed my arm, my biceps would show, and my abdomen was starting to get slightly defined.

"When I look at myself in the mirror, it almost feels like I'm looking at someone else entirely. I need to swap out all my shirts and suits, too..."

"Do you intend to continue with your work aboveground? The dungeon by itself should be more than sufficient to allay all of your financial burdens, should it not?"

Akane's words were reasonable. Unfortunately, that view was a bit too simplistic.

"For better or for worse, this world is an information society. If I suddenly own a large amount of money, the country would ask where I'd gotten that money. Small amounts for everyday use is fine, but large amounts are much harder to spend. In order to use the money that I earn from the dungeon, continuing my job aboveground is a necessity."

This dungeon dropped cold, hard cash. Small amounts wouldn't raise any eyebrows. The number of five hundred yen coins I currently owned was about four thousand, but that was still fine; I could still take it to the bank and exchange them for bills without much issue. The problem would be when that number climbed even higher. When it reached the millions, however, money without a clear origin became really hard to use.

"Should I try asking Iwa-chan for advice? If I remember correctly, real estate can be purchased with a lump sum of cash without having to provide income proof. I'll ask if he could introduce me to a lawyer, a tax counselor, and a realtor. I'm sure he's previously needed similar services while opening his pachinko parlors."

I took out my notebook and jotted down what had just come to mind. I now knew what I needed to do next.

◇ ◇ ◇

"I'm going to kill one hundred goblins to familiarize myself with the spear first. Then we'll go down to Floor 2."

I walked out into (onto?) Floor 1, holding the UC steel spear that I had obtained through gacha. The moment a goblin spawned, I stabbed it in its forehand or chest and promptly reduced it to smoke. I practiced brandishing the spear, both using one hand and using two hands. Before too long, I had finished off the intended hundred.

"Well then, let's hit Floor 2. Akane, take the front."

"As you wish, Kazuhiko-sama."

With the Glamorous Kunoichi taking the lead, we descended the stairs at the far end of Floor 1. When we had gone down what roughly felt like twenty meters, we arrived at a space that seemed like Floor 2.

"So there isn't a Safety Zone on this floor?"

"I'm sure there is one, but it's likely somewhere else. There should be a teleportation circle inside that is connected to the Safety Zone on Floor 1."

"...What a light-novel-like device."

As we continued our exchange, the two of us proceeded into Floor 2. At first glance, the interior looked the same as Floor 1, but the layout was no longer grid-like.

"For Floor 2 to already be a labyrinth layout... This dungeon definitely

lives up to its ranking. That said, it's absolutely meaningless before me. Ah, I feel a monster coming close."

The bewitching smile on Akane's face quickly turned into a grim look as the monster came into sight. The extremely muscular build with gray-brown skin that towered two meters high and walked on two legs was the spitting image of an orc.

"An orc?! A Rank D monster on Floor 2?!"

"MUUUAAAARRRRR!"

The instant the monster laid eyes on Akane, it charged forward with both arms outstretched. It did not possess a weapon, but the bulge below its waist was undoubtedly a weapon in a different sense.

"How filthy!"

Akane leaped up from the ground and kicked off of the walls. She reached the air above the orc almost instantaneously, then plunged a kunai straight into its head without hesitation. The orc's eyes rolled back even as it vanished into a puff of smoke. Even so, Akane's expression remained dark despite the fight being over.

"Kazuhiko-sama, this is an unexpected turn of events. With Floor 1 being occupied by Rank F goblins, I had expected to encounter Rank E monsters on Floor 2. For Rank D orcs to come out instead and skip over Rank E entirely is just..."

"It's fine. This works as well. If I gacha with Rank D monster cards, the difference, if there's any, should become all the more obvious. I'll try taking on the next orc that we encounter."

"Please hold on, Kazuhiko-sama! It's too dangerous. Orcs possess such superior strength that they can easily beat a human to death. To make matters worse, they do possess some measure of intelligence. The reason why they do not wield weapons is because they have no need to."

Akane attempted to stop me, but I had no intention of listening to her warning, as I had laid eyes on what had been dropped by the orc that had just been turned to smoke. Slowly, a one thousand yen bill floated down to the stone-paved ground.

"It appears that these orcs drop one thousand yen bills. Killing one hundred of them yields ¥100,000. The more I fight, the stronger I become as well. I can probably also look forward to the gacha rewards. We'll be pressing on. I'll take the next one."

Reluctantly, Akane nodded in acquiescence. Soon enough, another orc showed up. I stepped forward, bringing my three-meter spear to bear. First, I would stab its stomach, then aim for its forehead. So thinking, I lunged with the spear. However...

"MUAR!"

The orc easily slapped away my spear, then threw a fist at me with incredible speed. I barely managed to block it in time, but still ended up being blown away. I slammed against the far wall, suffering what was likely a cerebral concussion.

"Kazuhiko-sama!"

Akane's voice was the last thing that registered before I lost consciousness.

◇ ◇ ◇

I felt myself being made to drink something. Soon enough, I registered a voice calling out my name. When I slowly opened my eyes, Akane's worried face loomed into view. So I'm still in the dungeon.

"Kazuhiko-sama! Are you all right?!"

"I... Yeah, I'm fine. You gave me a potion?"

The pain from when I had slammed against the wall was gone. A quick check, and I realized that my wounds were gone, too.

"Please forgive me. I ended up using two of them."

"No, no, you saved me. That was a good call."

Akane was on her knees and prostrating herself in apology, so I patted her head and placed a hand on her cheek. Her shapely face abruptly flushed red, but we couldn't very well continue this romantic moment forever. There was no telling when the next orc would turn the corner. I stood up and returned the steel spear to card form.

"My weapon choice was a mistake. This long and spindly thing isn't suitable here. For orcs, this is what I need."

With a poof, I materialized the Club Card.

◇ ◇ ◇

"MUUUAAARRRRR!"

I ducked underneath the orc's punch, then slammed my club into its knee, shattering it. The monster crumpled to the ground, and I brought my weapon down onto its head. It wouldn't die with one or two strikes, so I swung down again and again while half in a trance. Eventually, the orc disappeared and turned into cash.

"Yep, this really is the correct way to fight these guys. As they don't hold any weapons, they have a strong tendency to throw big punches while relying on their superior strength. The most important thing when throwing a punch is the legs, especially how the big toe is planted. With one knee gone, these orcs' punches can't even hurt a fly. However, there are times when they start with a kick instead of a punch, so further testing is still needed."

Several days after I switched to using a club, I was still in the middle of working out the best way to kill orcs by continuing to pit myself against them one at a time. One, go through the physical experience. Two, mull over it and understand it. Lastly, derive laws and lessons from the whole process. This commonly adopted process for learning something in the business world was proving useful here in the dungeon as well. As I was now focusing more on improving my fighting style instead of meeting a quota, I took all the time I needed with each fight.

"This is extraordinary progress, Kazuhiko-sama! At this rate, we might be able to move on to Floor 3 soon!"

Akane and I were in the middle of reflecting over today's fights while spooning curry rice into our mouths. This place was not a game. This world did not have forgiving mechanics like getting stronger through level ups from accumulating XP. As so, we needed to set out clear and achievable goals, always keep efficiency and quality in mind during the enactment phase, and then make time for a proper reflection at the end of the process. This was something done by pretty much every single businessman who was worth his salt.

"No, I plan on remaining on Floor 2 for a while longer. We'll stay here at least until I reach Rank D."

"So the next goal is to reach human limits, I see. I shall do all I can to support you."

Of the ranks, F, E, and D were considered within human limits. F was a common person, E was an athlete, and D was the rare martial arts grandmaster or legendary warrior. To put things into perspective, this meant that Lü Bu and Tsukahara Bokuden were probably both Rank D.

After cleaning off my third plate of curry rice, I reached out for my bottle of supplements. Although Enhancement Element induced bodily strengthening, it alone was not sufficient to make me strong. Nutrients like protein, calcium, and vitamins were also crucial to the process. It was nigh impossible to maintain a healthy diet down in the dungeon, which was why I was taking supplements to make up for what I was missing. "As for you, you've already reached Rank D."

-------------------------------------------------------------------

Name: Akane

Title: Glamorous Kunoichi

Rank: D

Rarity: Legend Rare

Skills: Kunai Mastery (Lvl. 4), Enemy Detection (Lvl. 4), Sex Technique (Lvl. 4)

-------------------------------------------------------------------

The reason why Sex Technique had gone up was, well, you know, "adult reasons." I had had no intention of rejecting the advances of such a glamorous and stunningly beautiful woman forever; I wasn't that old yet. I guess it could also be said that my survival instinct had been kicked into gear by my life-and-death fights against the orcs. As for how the experience went..."it was wonderful" is the only thing I will say.

"I am a character card that's inherently part of the Dungeon System. I naturally get stronger just by absorbing Enhancement Element. When I'm by

your side, I feel like SSS is not just a dream but an eventuality."

Akane was a Legend Rare card, the highest rarity ranking among all the cards. There were only a total of 108 LR cards, and apparently they were all character cards. Exactly where they could be obtained was entirely uncertain. Supposedly, some could be traded for with the Peddler who would be appearing after the Dungeon System became fully activated, whereas there were others that could be found by chance inside unexplored dungeons.

"As for the current card drop rate of these Rank D orcs, it's roughly around 1%, which leads me to guess that this number is also affected by the monster's rank and my rank. In this case, because the orcs' rank is higher than mine, the drop rate is lower than it's supposed to be."

"However, Kazuhiko-sama, you are growing stronger at an accelerated rate. Surely it won't be that long until you rise up to Rank D. And now you look much younger again, almost as if you haven't aged a day past thirty."

Instead of getting all bulky like a bodybuilder, I could feel that my muscles had gotten incredibly dense. It was almost as if my body had been rebuilt from the most fundamental building blocks.

"Well then, let's go for another round. As always, it'll be one hundred goblins first, then Floor 2." "As you command."

I shouldered my club, signaling the end of our break.

◇ ◇ ◇

One hour aboveground was 144 hours - which equated to six days - inside the dungeon. Adding in the time that I needed to come back up for showers and to restock, the time conversion that I was aiming for was more like three aboveground hours for six dungeon days. As a management consultant, I still had to visit my clients at their places of business. Therefore, on my work days, I would only dive into the dungeon for about three to four hours, and then spend the rest of the day at home. Thanks to me doing all my work inside the dungeon, I had plenty of free time.

"The drop rewards that I am now earning from six dungeon days ranges between ¥1.6 million to ¥1.7 million. That's a daily profit of ¥1.5 million after subtracting ¥100,000 for costs like energy and food. Even if I was to take the occasional day off, I could still easily exceed ¥50 million in a month. The question, however, is how I can actually use this money. If I really brought hundreds of thousands to exchange at the bank week after week, that's definitely going to set alarm bells off. Considering the denomination of the bills, I'd have to declare it as income from a store, but I don't actually have a store."

Chances were high that this world was going to be obliterated in eleven years' time. Putting things in that perspective, the idea of properly paying my taxes ended up seeming quite inconsequential. Even so, I still had to come up with a way that I could use all this money. In order to prevent world destruction, I needed to gather companions. There was no way that I could clear all 666 dungeons by myself. Capital was necessary both for gathering companions and for setting up a base of operations.

"Once I reach Rank D, I'll pick up the Inducement skill. With the help of this skill, I'll go around buying up all the homes nearby. Then I'll have all of them razed, including my own, and build a huge facility that will also include residential living spaces. There, I will set up a company that specializes in dungeon delving, and use the power of that company to ensure that every single dungeon all over the world gets cleared."

For the moment, the exchange machines at banks could still suffice. Another option was to ask Iwamoto to exchange the bills for me. He ran pachinko parlors, and I've heard tell that five hundred yen coins and one thousand yen bills are the most frequently used denomination at those kinds of establishments. It would be a deal that would both save me trouble and work out to his benefit. If need be, I was even willing to pay a handling charge.

"What I need to focus on now is securing a way to convert my dungeon income into 'clean money' and set up a company specializing in clearing dungeons. When my rank goes up, I believe my income will go up as well."

I placed one thousand yen bills worth a total of ¥3 million into the safe, then headed off for my bedroom.

◇ ◇ ◇

"Sure, we can exchange the cash for you. It'd save us the trouble and processing fees from getting our own small denomination bills. And as for the realtor...there is one that we work with who even helps negotiate the purchase price and all that, but they do charge quite a bit of commission. That okay with you?"

"Sure, that works. As long as I can make all the purchases with a single cash payment."

"I'm asking just in case, but that cash isn't dirty money, right?"

"It's not money from doing anything illegal. Hmm... What would you do if you discovered a cave that spits out an endless stream of money like the magic mallet Uchide-no-Kozuchi?"

"Now that's an unexpected question coming from you. It almost sounds like the premise of an anime. Well...if it happened to me, I would first confirm whether that cash was real or not. Then, regardless of whether it's real or counterfeit, I'd report it to the police."

I smiled faintly while shrugging my shoulders. This friend of mine, Iwamoto, had an honest and upright personality. I had expected him to answer along those lines. However, apparently he still had more to say.

"If there were circumstances which made it impossible to report this to the police or let the public know, then I'd ignore said cave. If that cave cannot be ignored, I cannot simply discard the money, and I'm bound or compelled to use that money in some way... Well, there aren't a lot of options, really. The worst thing to do would be to report it as taxable income as is. It would depend on the amount, but that's basically just asking to be discovered. Money that's just flowing out can't be treated as lost property, so you wouldn't be able to legally lay claim to it three months later. In that case, then the best thing would be to just use it. If it's just several tens of thousands, no one would probably notice. If it's in the millions, however...using that much cash isn't going to be easy."

Iwamoto's words prompted me to heave a sigh. Guess it's going to be difficult after all. Just as I was about to give up and resign myself to using my money bit by bit, my friend looked away and started muttering to himself.

"If I ever find myself in such a situation, I'd probably hire a professional money launderer. After the money is rendered untraceable after being bounced around thousands of times between private banks and cryptocurrency markets, it can then be deposited into my bank account as consulting fees. I do, after all, know several such professionals currently residing in Japan."

To the very end, Iwamoto kept up the pretense of talking to himself even as he threw out keywords indicating that he would introduce me to one such professional and hashed out the smaller details like names and contact information. As someone who managed pachinko parlors, he had probably ended up with such underground connections even without seeking them. Iwamoto himself disliked using such methods and had been actively phasing them out of his company through the hotel side of things ever since he assumed his post. I was sure that if we hadn't been friends of over thirty years, he wouldn't have made such a risk. I simply lowered my head without saying anything.

◇ ◇ ◇

The meetup location turned out to be the parking lot of a building unrelated to Iwamoto's establishments. I entered the way I had been instructed to. There was only one specific parking space that was in a blind spot of the security cameras. I got into the back of the car parked in that spot. A slightly shrill voice - clearly altered with a voice changer - addressed me from the driver's seat.

"For amounts over ¥100 million, we keep 10% as commission. We'll launder the rest, and transfer it into your specified account as consulting fees from various companies. Online banks like Japan Web Bank are best for this kind of thing. Prepare one."

"As I'll be declaring this as taxable income, there is a possibility that shell corporations might get exposed. Are you all covered on that front?"

"Not a problem. All our corporations are real companies with healthy records. You don't have to know what our relationship with those companies is, and neither do you need to know what we'll be doing with the commission."

In all likelihood, it'd be going towards missile tests being conducted in a certain country. After mulling over it for a while, I decided to sign the contract after all. As things stood, humanity was going to be wiped out ten years from now. If being complicit with "evil" was the only way to avoid the worst-case scenario, then I had no choice...or at least, that was what I told myself. I promised to get in touch after setting up an account with an online bank, then made my exit.

◇ ◇ ◇

Almost a whole month had gone by since I first stepped foot inside Abyss. The number of orcs that I had killed was now only slightly shy of twenty thousand, which meant I had gathered more than one hundred Orc Cards. Therefore, it was about time for me to confirm how these would perform in the Card Gacha.

"Well then, here goes. Status Open."

-------------------------------------------------------------------

Name: Ezoe Kazuhiko

Title: First Contacter

Rank: E

Possession Limit: 200 / ∞

Skills: Card Gacha (22), Recovery Magic (Lvl. 2), ______, ______, ______,______

-------------------------------------------------------------------

The plan was to first roll with one hundred Goblin Cards, then one hundred Orc Cards. The purpose of this experiment was to verify whether the rarity of the cards used would affect the rewards that came out.

"Starting with the Goblin Cards now."

"You plan to spend all eleven rolls on the Item Gacha?"

Naturally, Item Gacha was the only way to go. At this point in time, I felt no need to change my weapon nor equipment, and neither did I plan on getting a monster servant. During the past month, it was item cards such as Potion Cards that I had ended up consuming the most. Potions had also proved helpful in helping me gauge the effect of my Recovery Magic.

I selected "Item Gacha" on my Status screen and rolled it eleven consecutive times. As expected, I got a lot of Commons, but there were a few Uncommons mixed in as well. The UCs were all repeats, though, so I'm only introducing them once.

-------------------------------------------------------------------

Name: High Potion

Rarity: Uncommon

Description: A highly potent potion that is effective even against bone-deep wounds and brain damage.

-------------------------------------------------------------------

"From the eleven rolls, I got three UCs and eight Cs. Considering the margin of error, the distribution seems to be unchanged from last time. Well then, time for the Orc Cards. We're talking Rank F against Rank D here; there's got to be a difference."

Secretly, there was quite a bit of expectation in my heart. It quickly crossed my mind that perhaps it was this expectation that kept so many people addicted to gacha and loot boxes in video games. I almost felt like I was about to buy a lottery ticket.

The result of the rolls turned out to be just as I had predicted. Below are the cards with a rarity of UC and higher that we were seeing for the first time.

-------------------------------------------------------------------

Name: High Magi Potion

Rarity: Uncommon

Description: Recovers more mana than a magi potion. Tasteless and odorless.

-------------------------------------------------------------------

Name: Single Use Barrier

Rarity: Uncommon

Description: Can be used to erect a barrier within a dungeon that keeps monsters out. Single use only.

-------------------------------------------------------------------

Name: Jointly Sealed Covenant

Rarity: Uncommon

Description: A covenant that binds both signed parties to the terms of one specific promise. Impossible to defy. Cannot be subverted by signing with an alias, as this item's effect is applied to the signers themselves.

-------------------------------------------------------------------

Name: Magic Pouch

Rarity: Uncommon

Description: A leather pouch with a storage capacity of ten cubic meters. Time inside the storage flows the same as outside.

-------------------------------------------------------------------

Name: Lucky Ring

Rarity: Uncommon

Description: Increases the wearer's luck by just a little bit. Possibly effective on drop rates.

-------------------------------------------------------------------

Name: Ufufu Lotion

Rarity: Uncommon

Description: Lotion for use by adult men and women. Very effective healing effect. Single use.

-------------------------------------------------------------------

Name: Drop-Rate Up Band

Rarity: Rare

Description: Increases drop rate of monster cards by 10%. Effective just from having it on your person.

-------------------------------------------------------------------

"As I had thought! Akane, look at this. The difference between the rewards from using Goblin Cards and Orc Cards is plain as day!" I cried, elated both from my hypothesis having been proven and from the unexpectedly great returns. "For Rank F cards, the reward distribution is 80% C and 20% UC. For Rank D cards, it seems to be 20% C, 70% UC, and 10% R. By inference, that means the distribution for Rank E cards is probably roughly half and half between C and UC. Perhaps Rank C cards would be half and half between UC and R."

I delightedly turned to input the results of the experiment into my spreadsheet software. Akane had surreptitiously slipped one card away, but I pretended like I hadn't seen it. It's been a while; guess I should get the air mattress ready.

◇ ◇ ◇

It was now almost a month in aboveground time since I had been first summoned. My Master, Kazuhiko-sama, had been very proactively diving into the dungeon. Thanks to this, he had quickly reached Rank E, after which he finally became receptive to my advances.

Kazuhiko-sama was someone who attached great importance to plans and calculations. He was now doing four-hour blocks of fighting, where he would kill one hundred goblins first - which he could manage under an hour now - and then tally up how many orcs he could kill in the remaining time. Whereas he had started out extremely cautious while fighting against the orcs, as he gradually got used to the task, in this, too, he had begun to place emphasis on speed. After around thirteen hours of fighting, he would then take a shower and rest up together with me in the Safety Zone on Floor 1.

For every 144 hours in the dungeon, Kazuhiko-sama would return to his work aboveground. In order to maintain his sense of time, he also made a point to get rest up there as well. With his spreadsheet program, he was constantly managing his time and his results, attempting to unlock secrets about the workings of the Dungeon System that even I did not know. The most overt example of this was, of course, his examination of the Card Gacha skill.

Although my memories had been wiped clean, as a character card of Legend Rare rarity, I held certain knowledge about the Dungeon System. Even so, I knew nothing about the existence of such a skill. At first glance, a skill that could exchange monster cards would seem extremely useful, but after all the effort spent gathering so many cards, the reward turned out to be a common potion. Even Kazuhiko-sama despaired at the outcome.

"The rarity of the cards used for Card Gacha should affect the rewards!"

This theory that Kazuhiko-sama touted did indeed seem likely. I was not privy to the details, but I knew that the Dungeon System was autonomous and self-learning. It was very likely listening even to every word exchanged between me and Kazuhiko-sama. Through this, it sought to understand the world that it had appeared in, all so that it could create the features and skills to match. A brand new skill created in this way would never be hackneyed and simplistic.

After defeating ten thousand orcs, Kazuhiko-sama used his Card Gacha skill once again. The rewards this time surprised me greatly. A High Potion was an extremely effective item. There were also items that I had never seen before, one of which immediately drew my eye. Thinking of how useful it would be for giving pleasure to Kazuhiko-sama, I surreptitiously sneaked the card into my pocket. It appeared that he had noticed, but said nothing. I took that to mean that he had given his permission. Master, I am a bad kunoichi who can't keep my fingers to myself. As atonement, please allow me to give you the best time ever with this UC card tonight!

◇ ◇ ◇

Slightly more than a month after the first dungeon had appeared in Shishibone, Edogawa City, Tokyo, or to be more precise, 3,155,760 seconds after the activation of the Rank A dungeon Abyss, a total of sixty-seven caves large enough for people to walk into appeared in large metropolitan hubs all over the world, including London, Paris, New York, Chicago, Osaka, Sydney, Seoul, and Beijing. This was the start to what would later be named the "Worldwide Synchronized Dungeon Outbreak Phenomenon."

The exact locations of the dungeons varied greatly, ranging from underground parking lots to smack-dab in the middle of intersections. Fearing the ensuing chaos, each country's government swiftly moved to keep a lid on the matter. However, in this information age, if a dungeon had appeared in the middle of the street, hiding its existence was an exercise in futility. It took less than a week before news of the "so-called dungeons" spread throughout the world. With the advent of the fantastical in this world built upon science, many went wild with enthusiasm, but even more were simply apprehensive.

What was going to become of this world going forward? At this point in time, there was but a single man who had even the slightest inkling.

Chapter 2: The Dungeon Outbreak Phenomenon

"GAMERICA FIRST!"

President Ronald Howard of the United States of Gamerica, the world's foremost military and economic power, was a man who had gotten elected to his position based on a platform of putting Gamerica first. He was a hardliner when it came to foreign policy, and there were those who thought of him as a tyrant, but he was by no means a man without common sense. He was one to say what he wanted to say and hear what he needed to hear.

"Well, who are these stupid people who have launched an attack on our incredible nation?"

The president's question caused everyone else present to exchange looks.

After clearing his throat, the secretary of defense spoke up.

"Mr. President, to be precise, we are not under attack. It's just that two caves have appeared, within which time flows differently. No enemy soldiers have come out of those caves, and we have suffered no casualties. However, there are preliminary reports of aggressive unknown creatures inside those caves, which we are still confirming at the moment."

"What do you mean 'time flows differently'? How different is it?"

"It appears to be by a factor somewhere between 140 and 150. As time increasingly grows faster the deeper we go in, we have yet to pinpoint the exact number," answered the vice president.

President Howard crossed his arms, then issued orders.

"In any case, there must be a reason why these unrealistic-sounding caves have appeared. Investigate them thoroughly. And don't let the people know yet. Get in touch with other countries, and figure out what's the deal with these caves ASAP."

Despite his instructions to not let the people know, this president had a tendency to "accidentally" leak important information through his social media account. Although those present at the briefing immediately went off to carry out the president's orders, they all knew it was only a matter of time before the news got out.

◇ ◇ ◇

The prime minister of Japan's official residence, called the Kantei, was located at 2-3-1 Nagata-chou, Chiyoda City, Tokyo. This day saw the ninetyeighth prime minister of Japan, Urabe Seiichirou, frowning at the photo that he had just been handed. The cabinet ministers, who had all been summoned for an extraordinary meeting, all tilted their heads in equal bewilderment.

In his characteristic Tokyo Shitamachi dialect, the minister of finance, who was an avid manga reader, said, "Dogs that walk on two legs? That sounds awfully similar to kobolds in manga. Are we looking at light novels come to life?"

However, in this room of mostly men over sixty years old, there weren't many who understood what he was referring to. The chief cabinet secretary cleared his throat.

"Ahem. So, the location where the cave in question has appeared is an underground parking lot inside the Umeda district of Osaka. One week earlier, the local police force received reports of the cave, and two policemen went inside, where they were assaulted by the strange creatures depicted in the photos in everyone's hands. Sergeant Satou Kouji of Sonezaki Police

Station was killed in the line of duty, and his partner suffered severe injuries. According to the survivor's testimony, when the two of them found themselves under attack and reached for their guns, they discovered that their weapons had been converted into what seemed like cards. At the time, his testimony was held under doubt, but what was certain was that he had lost his gun while escaping. The day before yesterday, a riot squad was sent in, but true to the above testimony, they found all their guns and batons converted into cards. They were then assaulted by the strange creatures wielding daggers. There were no fatalities, thankfully, but many in the squad were severely injured."

"Is there any possibility of this being a terrorist attack?" asked Prime Minister Urabe.

The National Public Safety Commision chairman stood up and said,

"There has been no movement from any of the religious cults or left-wing organizations under our surveillance. Even if this was a terrorist attack, it's hard to imagine the intention behind such a large-scale operation..."

The minister of defense added, "And that wouldn't explain the caves that have also appeared in other countries."

The whole room was set astir. These past few days, video-hosting sites had been flooded with uploads with the word "dungeon" in the title, and almost all of these had come from places other than Japan. If this was truly a phenomenon that had occurred throughout the entire world at the same time, then it was very unlikely to be a terrorist attack. However, that would then leave the possibility of this being a mysterious new catastrophe of much greater scale and with much greater consequences.

"We've received an inquiry from Gamerica through the commanding officer of the U.S. forces stationed in Japan. They want to know whether we've had any strange caves appearing on our side. According to the contacts I have inside the U.S. government, caves similar to the one in Osaka have

also appeared in New York and Chicago."

"Any information from the Ministry of Foreign Affairs?"

"Not at the moment, no... I'll check in with the ASEAN countries, too."

Prime Minister Urabe nodded at the foreign minister's suggestion, then turned to address the room at large.

"All departments, be cautious with your investigations. If this is a terrorist plot, then it can only have been carried out by an enormous international organization that we have yet to even hear of. But in that case, we would still be dealing with humans. If this isn't a terrorist plot, if this really is a mysterious new natural disaster..."

"Then we wouldn't be able to prevent a panic, I imagine. Guess I'll go reread a few light novels when I get back. I seem to remember there being a few series with similar settings under the Low Fantasy category on the

Shousetsuka ni Narou site."

It took only a few days before it became apparent that the finance minister's words could no longer be passed off as a mere joke.

◇ ◇ ◇

"So it's finally started. The entire world's in a panic," I said while showing Akane videos that I had downloaded onto my tablet before coming down.

During the past week, the United Nations had called an emergency session, where heated discussion took place. Just now, UN headquarters had made an official announcement regarding the appearance of the dungeons. Namely, each country was to take responsibility for the dungeons that appear in its borders, and that all countries were to openly share all information they gather. A certain neighboring country with a huge population that had ended up with more than ten dungeons had apparently already begun pressing countries without dungeons for Official Development Assistance (ODA).

Rather than the international scene, however, there was another piece of news that I found more weighty: a policeman who had entered the dungeon at Osaka had died in the line of duty. When I first heard this news, a grimace came over my face. Being injured was one thing; potions could fix that. However, there was no way to bring back the dead. Because I had carelessly gone down the stairs that appeared in my yard and triggered this phenomenon, someone had died. It wasn't as if I could have done anything to prevent this, but I still could not help but to feel responsible somehow.

As if to distract myself, I laughed at the news that was playing on the tablet. "There are more and more voices expressing apprehension towards the appearance of the dungeons, but as expected, there are those making light of the situation. 'Open the dungeons to the general public!' they say. Why do they still want to enter, even though it's already been announced that weapons cannot be brought in? Are they thinking of fighting against orcs with their bare hands?"

"Such fools should just die. I cannot imagine them being of any use to you even when alive. Kazuhiko-sama, surely these are not the kinds of individuals that you are seeking as companions, right?"

"The companions that I want are those who possess a strong motivation to clear dungeons other than for personal gain. Ranking up is a very stressful process with a not-insignificant chance of death. Someone who's only doing it for personal gain will not be able to last long. It is only when fighting for someone else's sake that humans exhibit incredible emotional strength."

Akane leaned into me while running her fingers over a business card on my desk.

"And what an interesting organization it is that you are attempting to create to gather such companions. You continue to intrigue me more and more, Kazuhiko-sama..."

On the business card, the words "Dungeon Busters Inc." was written in a clear, bold font.

◇ ◇ ◇

During the past few weeks, in parallel with my efforts at ranking up and earning money, I had also been making preparations for the full activation of the Dungeon System that was supposedly coming one year later. The biggest thing was setting up a company that specialized in clearing dungeons. I registered "Dungeon Busters Inc." as the name, purchased trademark rights and the domain name for the eventual website, and set up email and social media accounts. For the trademark, I went the extra mile to register it as an international trademark. As the company was eventually going to clear dungeons in other countries as well, being thorough with these things beforehand was a necessity.

"For what it's worth, I even commissioned someone to design the logo for me."

It was a caricatured goblin behind a red cross-out mark like a "no parking" sign. The design was extremely simple, but that was what made it feel all the more "real." I had accepted it on the spot.

"Will you begin gathering companions now?"

"For now, I'll wait and see how each country responds to the dungeons. At the moment, ranking up is still my top priority. When I reached Rank D, more skills in the list had become visible. I take that to mean that even more of them will become unlocked when I reach Rank C. There's a certain skill that I absolutely want."

"Rank C is the first rank beyond human limits. I'm afraid it will take quite some time..."

-------------------------------------------------------------------

Name: Ezoe Kazuhiko

Title: First Contacter

Rank: D

Possession Limit: 1 / ∞

Skills: Card Gacha (0), Recovery Magic (Lvl. 3), Inducement (Lvl. 1), ______, ______, ______

-------------------------------------------------------------------

It was one week ago that I had finally broken through to Rank D. My body was completely different from what it had been a month ago, although it wasn't all that obvious underneath my suit. Both my grip strength and back strength had reached world-record levels. However, if asked whether I was strong or not, I wouldn't be able to give a straight answer. Just because my physical capabilities had gone up, it did not automatically translate into combat capability. I had lived all forty years of my life without any connection to violence. I did not know any martial arts, and I was but a novice at the sword and the spear.

-------------------------------------------------------------------

Name: Akane

Title: Glamorous Kunoichi

Rank: C

Rarity: Legend Rare

Skills: Kunai Mastery (Lvl. 5), Enemy Detection (Lvl. 4), Sex Technique (Lvl. 4)

-------------------------------------------------------------------

Akane's rank had also gone up, but the coward in me wanted to take things with a wide enough safety margin. At the moment, I was still fighting orcs with the club. When I became capable of consistently winning against them with my bare hands, that would be when I knew for sure that I had truly exceeded human limits.

"I'll continue training on Floor 2 for a while longer. In order to further increase my speed, strength, and stamina, I'll start wearing wrist weights, ankle weights, and a weight belt while fighting."

"Understood. But before that..."

Akane snuggled up to me with moist eyes. Perhaps because my body had turned young again, or perhaps because I was in an excited state due to the world acknowledging the existence of the dungeons, I, too, was in the mood. Without hesitation, I picked the Glamorous Kunoichi up and brought her to the bed.

◇ ◇ ◇

"HAH!"

One swing of my club, and the orc's head was pulverized. The orc fights that had used to take me several hits now only required two. After I reached Rank D, the drop rate for cards went up again, as I had expected. It was now 5% for the goblins on Floor 1, and 3% for the orcs on Floor 2. Thanks to the item Drop-Rate Up Band, these numbers were pushed up even higher. It was no longer that much of a chore gathering one hundred Orc Cards.

"I keep thinking this, but this Enhancement Element sure is an interesting thing. Normally, the more a human trains, the more muscle they gain. In other words, they bulk up.
